  <COMMENT line1="11" col1="1" line2="11" col2="78" start="1200" end="1277">#' sample. Putting more than one sample's results in the directory will result</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="19" col1="1" line2="19" col2="79" start="2072" end="2150">#' This function will work for Salmon v0.7.x and greater, as the name of one of</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="20" col1="1" line2="20" col2="74" start="2181" end="2254">#' the default output directories was changed from "aux" to "aux_info" in </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="21" col1="1" line2="21" col2="15" start="2290" end="2304">#' Salmon v0.7.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="22" col1="1" line2="22" col2="3" start="2399" end="2401">#' </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="23" col1="1" line2="23" col2="76" start="2508" end="2583">#' @return A list with two elements: (1) a data.frame \code{abundance} with </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="24" col1="1" line2="24" col2="78" start="2617" end="2694">#' columns for 'target_id' (feature, transcript, gene etc), 'length' (feature </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="25" col1="1" line2="25" col2="76" start="2726" end="2801">#' length), 'est_counts' (estimated feature counts), 'tpm' (transcripts per </COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="29" col1="1" line2="29" col2="73" start="3162" end="3234">#' number of reads that did not match the given or inferred library type,</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="253" col1="1" line2="253" col2="80" start="27578" end="27657">################################################################################</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="254" col1="1" line2="254" col2="58" start="27687" end="27744">#' Run Salmon on FASTQ files to quantify feature abundance</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="255" col1="1" line2="255" col2="2" start="27796" end="27797">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="256" col1="1" line2="256" col2="72" start="27905" end="27976">#' Run the abundance quantification tool \code{Salmon} on a set of FASTQ</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="257" col1="1" line2="257" col2="78" start="28014" end="28091">#' files. Requires \code{Salmon} (\url{https://combine-lab.github.io/salmon/})</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="258" col1="1" line2="258" col2="79" start="28123" end="28201">#' to be installed and a Salmon transcript index must have been generated prior</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="259" col1="1" line2="259" col2="76" start="28232" end="28307">#' to using this function. See the Salmon website for installation and basic</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="260" col1="1" line2="260" col2="22" start="28341" end="28362">#' usage instructions.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="261" col1="1" line2="261" col2="2" start="28450" end="28451">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="262" col1="1" line2="262" col2="79" start="28559" end="28637">#' @param targets_file character string giving the path to a tab-delimited text</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="263" col1="1" line2="263" col2="80" start="28668" end="28747">#' file with either 2 columns (single-end reads) or 3 columns (paired-end reads)</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="264" col1="1" line2="264" col2="80" start="28777" end="28856">#' that gives the sample names (first column) and FastQ file names (column 2 and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="265" col1="1" line2="265" col2="79" start="28886" end="28964">#' if applicable 3). The file is assumed to have column headers, although these</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="266" col1="1" line2="266" col2="16" start="28995" end="29010">#' are not used.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="267" col1="1" line2="267" col2="73" start="29104" end="29176">#' @param transcript_index character string giving the path to the Salmon</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="268" col1="1" line2="268" col2="61" start="29213" end="29273">#' index to be used for the feature abundance quantification.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="269" col1="1" line2="269" col2="77" start="29322" end="29398">#' @param single_end logical, are single-end reads used, or paired-end reads?</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="270" col1="1" line2="270" col2="80" start="29431" end="29510">#' @param output_prefix character string giving the prefix for the output folder</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="271" col1="1" line2="271" col2="75" start="29540" end="29614">#' that will contain the Salmon results. The default is \code{"output"} and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="272" col1="1" line2="272" col2="80" start="29649" end="29728">#' the sample name (column 1 of \code{targets_file}) is appended (preceded by an</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="273" col1="1" line2="273" col2="15" start="29758" end="29772">#' underscore).</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="274" col1="1" line2="274" col2="71" start="29867" end="29937">#' @param lib_type scalar, indicating RNA-seq library type. See Salmon </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="275" col1="1" line2="275" col2="70" start="29976" end="30045">#' documentation for details. Default is "A", for automatic detection.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="276" col1="1" line2="276" col2="71" start="30085" end="30155">#' @param n_processes integer giving the number of processes to use for</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="277" col1="1" line2="277" col2="77" start="30194" end="30270">#' parallel Salmon jobs across samples. The package \code{parallel} is used. </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="278" col1="1" line2="278" col2="37" start="30303" end="30339">#' Default is 2 concurrent processes.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="279" col1="1" line2="279" col2="78" start="30412" end="30489">#' @param n_thread_per_process integer giving the number of threads for Salmon</COMMENT>
